Pitou French Twill Japanese Goods Sell Well

The sales of French twill are currently at their most prosperous time. Thick wool coats all need to be lined with it, and the selling price is also at its best. Recently, with the influx of Japanese goods, prices have reversed and decreased. The Ai 277 brand has already dropped from 5 jiao to 4 jiao and 8 and a half fen, because 20 packages of Japanese French twill were imported last week, and the price per yard dropped from 4 jiao to 3 jiao and 7 fen. Most Western-style tailors are purchasing and using it, so the Ai 277 brand has also had to lower its price. However, the selling price of domestic French twill remains unchanged. Hongsheng goods are still sold at 4 jiao, and miscellaneous second-grade goods are sold at 4 yards per package.

Hardware Galvanized Iron Tile Bottom Goods in a Panic

Galvanized iron tiles are necessary for building houses. Large warehouses and railway buildings all need to use them. Every time the plum rain season arrives, the outlet for this product is sure to be very prosperous. However, this year, it is the exact opposite, because the weather is dry, and the market in various places is not good, so the outlet has suffered a major blow. The goods that various firms have pre-ordered are arriving one after another, and there is a worry of being full of goods. Standard Bank, although traders are trying to maintain it, but it finally goes downstream. At this time, those who hold goods suffer severely, and dare not order goods at all, so no spot goods have arrived since April and May. However, the local inventory is sold daily and monthly, and the bottom goods are in short supply. Therefore, those who want to order from each industry have a sigh of being unable to buy goods. Now I will record the various colors below.

(No. 24) Although the inventory of this product is still relatively abundant, the cost is extremely large, so traders are extremely unwilling to lower the price, and there is no sign of a decrease. The price is estimated at 11 yuan and 4 jiao per load. It is estimated that over 200 loads were traded yesterday, which were dismantled from Hongkou. It is heard that they were bought by the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Engineering Department. The market inventory is still 2,780 loads. If no goods arrive within the year, it is feared that it will also be out of stock next spring.

(No. 26) This product is already out of stock on the market. It is estimated that only Yitiehang and Xinrenchang Hardware Store are holding this product. The market price is estimated at 12 yuan and 6 jiao and a half per load, which is 2 jiao and a half better than the previous day. It is heard that buyers are still absorbing, and the trend is continuing to improve.

(No. 28) Yesterday, various firms in Hankou and Qingdao all made purchases, and the local factories also saw good activity. The market price is 13 yuan and 5 jiao per load, which is also 1 jiao firmer than before. The inventory is also very scarce, and it looks like it will improve again.

Spring and Autumn

Little Western Heaven

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter Six: A Poor Woman Can't Be Different, So She's Allowed to Teach, Looking at the Western Teacher as an Equal, Not Enough, Empty Insult, Empty Heart

Jia Duocai felt that for such a refugee woman, her value was no more than that of an insect. To love her and shower her with affection, or to hate her and sink her into the abyss, it didn't matter. However, these two Germans coming to visit was not something to be taken lightly. It wasn't necessarily that he valued the Germans so much, but because having foreigners come to visit could raise his own status. It was often said that foreigners looked down on Chinese people, so a special, admiring visit meant that they thought highly of him, and that elevated his status. Thinking this way, he couldn't help but be extremely happy. He immediately took it upon himself to tidy the teapots, teacups, and cigarette holders on the table, arranging them neatly on a small table to the side. He opened his suitcase, took out a white cloth bundle to spread on the table, creating a tablecloth. He also placed a wire basket and stacked a few old Chinese novels in Western binding on the corner of the table. Since he didn't have things like a fountain pen or blue ink in his temporary quarters, he put a few pencils and Western-style envelopes beside the books to create the impression of an office setup and a scholarly atmosphere. However, just a few books weren't enough to show how great his learning was, so he opened his suitcase again and took out the forms that the bank had ordered him to fill out, placing them on the table as well. Fortunately, these were all in Chinese characters, which could awe the foreigners for a while. How would they know what the contents were? After making these preparations, he called the tea boy to sweep the floor and dust the bedding. Only then did he sit down calmly and murmur a few English phrases he had learned more than ten years ago, such as "How do you do," reciting them to himself. Fortunately, they were Germans, and their English probably wouldn't be very good either. As long as he could handle a few sentences himself to show that he could also speak a foreign language, that would be enough. As he was practicing his diplomatic etiquette in the room, he heard a series of mixed-up leather shoe sounds outside the window. He thought that these must be the foreign guests, so he calmed down and waited quietly for them to enter. (96)

Remnants

— By Chen Liang

Because I am also a member of the weak in this world, I symbolize with the lament and elegy of people for the miserable insect chirping. However, the insect noises have long been silent, and only the cold wind is demonstrating outside the paper window. This is a cold and serious season! When the morning dew solidifies into frost, all insects are either frozen to death or hibernating. However, in my chaotic small building, there is still a "Call Brother" hiding in the paper-covered bamboo strips. Regarding the remnants of insects, from childhood until now, I have had a heart that cherishes small insects.

I remember that the summer, which was suitable for the survival of "Call Brother," had passed. It still remained under the eaves of Yinggu's house. When the afternoon sunlight shone on the window screen for a moment, I would always hear that remnant faint life fluttering its wings and making a desperate wail in her house while reading books or newspapers, slowly crawling in the bamboo cage, and occasionally extending two front legs out of the empty cracks. The emerald green wings had turned brown. 'Can't you extend its life a little longer? Find a way to rescue the weak from the harsh season!' I asked Yinggu to move it from under the eaves to the inner room, and then wrap it in a layer of leather paper to give it a suitable temperature.

Although Yinggu did what I said, she always laughed at me for being a little foolish, thinking that the life of something as small as an insect was not worth such care, and that the weak should only be destroyed in the environment (?).

The weather was getting colder day by day, and I could no longer hear the chirping of "Call Brother" in Yinggu's house. I opened the wrapped leather paper to look at the cage, and it stayed still like a specimen. Later, it quietly crawled again, but stopped again after a while. So, I knew that this tiny life would be destroyed sooner or later. I couldn't care about Yinggu's ridicule, and I wanted to take it to my own small building. I filled the cage with cotton and pasted two layers of leather paper around it, leaving only a small hole to let the air flow. I put it in a warm place, so that it could supposedly endure the coming winter.

It is now the progressive period of the cold and serious season, but there is still a weak insect hibernating in my chaotic small building. It is a comfort to me to transform the environment for the weak and extend their lives.

Odds and Ends

— (Boguang)

(Odds and Ends) Mr. ×× gave a speech advocating saving the country with homespun cloth and received enthusiastic applause from the audience. After the meeting, Mr. ×× returned home, saying he would take off his homespun cloth gown and put on a stylish Western suit and leather shoes to go on a date with his lover. This is the most brilliant person in Chinese society!

Central Committee member Wu Zhihui said, "Chinese people only have mouths and no butts; they can all talk but can't do." This sentence is really correct. (Boguang)

Fire Prison

— Lan Shan

"Isn't this a living hell on earth!"

Every time I passed by those blacksmith shops, I thought like this. No matter the season, their iron-smelting furnaces were always red. Although the furnace was red, everything else was black. The shop base was especially lower than others. When you sat down, the ground was completely black mud. The corners of the walls were piled with many iron rods and iron heads. The tables and chairs were mostly placed diagonally and haphazardly, as if they had been sprayed with black paint. When the experienced partner picked up a red-hot iron cake from the furnace and placed it on the iron pier, a young apprentice immediately came and hammered it in turns with a large hammer. Sparks flew into the air, falling on their feet and on the forehead of the apprentice who was sitting there pulling the bellows. Iron filings turned into dust, flying around everywhere. It was difficult to recognize everyone's faces. Coal dust replaced snow cream and skin care products, dyeing their hair, ears, eyes, noses, and mouths with a layer of gray-black mist. Fortunately, the weather is cold today, and working by this hot furnace is a good place to ward off the cold. You haven't seen their suffering in the scorching heat of summer - bare-chested and wearing shorts, their eyes emitting red light, coarse veins bulging on their faces, and sweat steaming from their bodies. Smoke ash and coal dust took the opportunity to attack and occupy everyone's bodies. That is suffering! That is living torment!

Now it is only the beginning of the cold season, but the hands of the young partners in the iron shop are already red and swollen. It's the same to make a living, but some are as happy as ascending to heaven, while others are as miserable as falling into hell. The entertainment venues of people do not have the footprints of this group of pitiful people, who only work hard and suffer in the fire prison all day long. When I pass by those iron shops, I always think uneasily for a while.

— Yi An

Fellows, we still have a hurdle to overcome

Thoughts

— Long Zhong

On an auspicious day, I sat at home and heard the passing musicians playing trumpets and drums on the street, making a lively sound. Walking on the street, I also saw more than a dozen red-letter lanterns lined up in front of the restaurants, their lights shining brightly, creating a great atmosphere. At this time, I suddenly wondered: how many good matches are made on each so-called auspicious day? How many unhappy couples are created? How many lovers happily become family members? And how many people's chastity will be violated? I remember that the Christian, Romulus, once said: "Marriage is at least a sin!" I feel that there is also great truth in that.

Seeing an advertisement in the newspaper for a company recruiting clerks, I thought again that this time, I don't know how many dozens, or even hundreds, of "bookworms" will taste the bitterness of disappointment!

Visiting the municipal zoo, I immediately had a thought: humans are also a kind of object. Why not lock them in iron cages and display them with foxes and monkeys? If a few criminals were locked up for citizens to visit, it would also be a very beneficial method.

I accidentally picked up a withered "Lily of the Valley" at the door, and I felt that life is too cruel and ruthless. A flower is like a young girl. I carefully wiped the abandoned "Lily of the Valley" with a silk scarf, put it in a small and exquisite brocade box, and wrote two hundred passionate words on the back of the brocade box to express my little bit of feeling.

World News

A Strange Tale of Kisses

— Huang Yingdai

A long time ago, I published an article called "An Anthology of Kisses" in Chunqiu. Recently, I found many more "Strange Tales of Kisses" in Western newspapers. Because they were very interesting, I gathered them together and wrote them below.

Kissing Fine A traveler who arrived in Moscow, Soviet Union, immediately encountered a surprising incident. Because he kissed his wife on the train, he was fined five pounds. He said that because she didn't feel very well, he intended to give her a few kisses to cheer her up. Unexpectedly, as soon as he finished kissing her, the military police on the train came to ask him for a fine. According to Soviet law, kissing on trains, in cars, or in public places is illegal and punishable? Whether the kissing couple is married or not, the punishment is the same. Moscow recently passed a law requiring all taxis to operate in well-lit areas.

Kissing Photography On the silver screen, we often see male and female stars embracing and kissing when they are expressing intense emotions. However, since the invention of sound films, which replaced silent films, kiss shots must now include the sound of the kiss, so they cannot be faked. Mae West is a very popular star in Hollywood. When she was filming a new movie, she had to shoot a kissing scene, and the first kiss had to have the sound of lips trembling. Everything was ready, and the director gave the command, "Miss Mae, kiss lightly." Mae then kissed the male lead. Who knew that the sound was too light. They tried again, but it was too heavy. They did countless kisses without getting the shot right. This really made Mae West furious. Finally, the director came up with the clever idea of ​​attaching a piece of silk to the microphone, and the kissing scene was finally filmed.

Kissing Love Letter A Mrs. Rice Brooke from Sydney wrote a letter to her lover in Estonia, along with a package. Because the letter contained the sentence "A thousand kisses to you," her husband sued for divorce. As for the package, it contained sausages. Her lover was called Kirk, and her letter read: "My dear Martin Kirk, I returned home safely. Shea was already awake. I know he must know that I was out all night. I am all yours, and all my thoughts revolve around you. A thousand kisses to you, my dear child. Now I'm sending you some sausages. Shea is watching me closely, and suddenly asked why I don't have a child. If these sausages aren't very good now, then just cook them for five minutes, and they will taste better." Kirk's reply: "I hope to see you in my dreams, your big child." Because of these two letters, the most important thing was "...a thousand kisses to you..." and the court ruled for divorce.

Kissing Enemies Since the beginning of history, love has occupied a large part of human life. Women live for love, men die for love, children are the crystallization of love, and most of the poems and novels written by poets and scholars focus on love. Even illiterate people will naturally sing folk love songs. After love matures between men and women, regardless of civilization or barbarism, there is a common formula, which is to express it with a kiss. Whether they are foolish men or foolish women, when they reach the peak of love, they will unconsciously embrace and kiss passionately. But there are exceptions. In North Africa, there are some ethnic groups where women do not know how to kiss. They will never kiss anyone until they die of old age. If a man wants to kiss them, they will treat him as an enemy, without a doubt. In this world, they may be the enemies of kissing.

Imperial Incense Floating Record

— Original by Princess Der Ling, Translated by Qin Shouou

But this fox's vanity is very heavy - vanity is not considered a bad habit. It felt that if it cut off its ninth tail, its inherent beauty would be completely lost, and how could it have the face to live on after that? Therefore, it was unwilling to suffer the punishment of tail cutting anymore. So it sincerely pleaded with the Jade Emperor, "From now on, I am thoroughly awakened - whatever you want me to do, I am willing to do my best, but please allow me to keep this last tail. Let me keep a little bit of dignity, and I will be eternally grateful to you. Please allow me to repent! From now until the day the world is destroyed, I will never dare to do any bad things again!" After such a tearful plea, the compassionate Jade Emperor couldn't help but feel compassion again - he lowered his head and thought for a long time, and finally came up with a solution. He said to the fox, "Your past sins are really too many, and logically you should not be pardoned. Now that you have shown sincere remorse, I will forgive you once more. This time, however, you cannot be as carefree as before! I will now assign you a job, teach you to carefully take on the responsibility of treating all kinds of human diseases, and appoint you as the God of Healing. The term of this job is nine thousand years. Because it is not such a long time, it cannot offset your previous sins!" The fox listened and readily agreed without any difficulty, so it retained its last tail. This tail represents the bad habit of infatuated admiration for beautiful women. This bad habit is already the worst of its original nine, and at the same time, it got the title of "Great Green Fox Immortal". (206)

Shen Bao Wireless Weekly

Homemade Lead-Acid Batteries

— Yongchang

It seems that no one has talked about the homemade production of storage batteries. Now I will introduce what I have learned through experience. The price of a storage battery is two or three yuan for a Class A battery and more than ten yuan for a Class B battery. If you can make it yourself, the total cost will be less than three yuan.

(1) Materials

Pure lead: Purchase from lead and tin shops or auto repair shops.

Sulfuric acid: Purchase from pharmacies, about four corners per pound. Lead dioxide: Also available from pharmacies, or use nitric acid and peach dan (purchase from Chinese pharmacies) and heat together to obtain a brown powder.

Pure lead powder: This powder is not easy to buy and can be replaced with mitoseng from Chinese pharmacies.

(2) Manufacturing

First, use a very thin piece of wood as a bottom template, and then make two clay molds. After the molds have hardened, carve many parallel grooves on the molds, with a gap of about half an inch between the grooves (as shown in the figure). Then put the two molds together and pour in molten lead. The finished lead plates will have protruding grid patterns on both sides. Make several of these lead cups.

Half of the lead plates are used as the positive electrode, and the grids are filled with a mixture of lead dioxide and sulfuric acid. Half are used as the negative electrode, and the grids are filled with pure lead powder, or a mixture of mitoseng and sulfuric acid. These two sets of lead plates are inserted into a glass container with intervals. Each cathode and anode must be separated by insulation. Finally, a mixture of one part sulfuric acid and ten parts distilled water (note: the sulfuric acid must be slowly poured into the distilled water; do not pour the distilled water into the sulfuric acid, otherwise there is a risk of explosion) is added to the glass bottle. Connect the cathode and anode plates in series to form the cathode and anode poles, and then seal the top with rosin to form a perfect storage battery.

The voltage of this storage battery is 108 volts when fully charged, and the current depends on the area of the plates. Approximately one ampere of current is generated for every twelve square inches of the area of the cathode and anode. Although the homemade storage battery is not as effective as the commercially available product, it is much cheaper. Readers, why not give it a try?

Latest Small Acorn Vacuum Tube

— Yisun

Recently, the American RCA company has announced the successful manufacture of small vacuum tubes, and these vacuum tubes are already on sale in the market. It is named RCA955A acorn tube, and the price is also quite cheap. The purpose of manufacturing this vacuum tube is to minimize the capacitance between the internal electrodes, especially for ultra-short wave reception, which will not cause various problems. It is also very effective for receiving broadcasts or other wavelengths.

Speaking of the size of this vacuum tube, it is only the size of an acorn, with a height of one and sixteen-sixteenths of an inch, and a width of only one inch (including the wiring terminals). The various properties of this vacuum tube are similar to those of the ordinary No. 37. It is also a triode, but with an indirectly heated cathode. The filament uses 6.3 volts for lighting and 0.16 amps. The capacitance between the screen and the grid is 1.4 mmfd, the capacitance between the grid and the cathode is mmre, and the capacitance between the screen and the cathode is 6mmjd, which can be said to be extremely small.

Substitute for Audio Frequency Choke

— Yongyan

In the filtering circuit of the B battery, the audio frequency choke coil is an indispensable component. However, the cost of an accurately designed, sturdy, and durable audio frequency choke coil is very high. For the sake of economy, we may as well use a substitute, which is the resistor we commonly use.

Using a resistor to replace the audio frequency choke coil seems to be slightly inferior in terms of blocking ability; but it also has considerable advantages. One: the cost is low; two: it occupies a very small area; three: the matching effect caused by the iron core of the audio frequency choke coil can be avoided after replacing it with a resistor.

The number of ohms of this resistor must be determined according to the vacuum tube in the machine, as long as it does not excessively reduce the B voltage. In ordinary two- or three-tube machines using 27 or 37 and other vacuum tubes, about 3,000 or 4,000 ohms are used. If the number of vacuum tubes is increased, the number of ohms can be reduced. If the machine has powerful audio frequency amplification, the number of ohms should be further reduced. The detailed number can be determined by testing. The number of watts of this resistor, ordinary one-watt, is not too hot, and three watts can also be used in a powerful audio frequency amplifier, and it is of course better to use a larger one.

Single-Tube Crystal Dual-Use Machine

— Cai Rixin

The A-141 tube is produced by Philips. Its structure is double-grid, dual-gate, with extremely high amplification, and very low cathode voltage. The B voltage used is only a dozen volts enough; so this vacuum tube is valued by amateurs. This article introduces a single-tube machine with excellent selectivity and superb volume. We know that the reason why crystal radio is eliminated is because it has the advantage of not using electricity. Adding a crystal to the circuit of this single-tube machine makes it a dual-use machine. The circuit diagram is as follows:

L1: 24-gauge wire, in the L1 coil.

L1: 26-gauge wire, wound 56 turns on the same.

L2: Wound 34 turns on the same. (The above are installed on a three-circuit frame)

C: .0005 microfarad variable capacitor.

Cc: .00025 microfarad fixed capacitor.

V: Philips A-141 tube.

D: Sensitive ore.

R: 20-ohm variable resistor.

R1: 2 megohm grid leak.

A: One and a half volts.

B: Twenty-two and a half or sixteen and a half volts.

Low-Frequency Amplification Coupling Circuit

— Liu Tongkang

(B) Resistance Coupling

As shown in Figure 3, this type of coupling method has been widely used since the prevalence of AC machines, because its advantages cannot be matched by transformer coupling. First, this type has no frequency characteristics, so the amplification performance for any frequency is extremely smooth and consistent; second, because there is no parallel resonance phenomenon, each frequency of speech and music can obtain equal amplification, so there is no distortion. In addition, because a tetrode is used for detection, its AC screen resistance is extremely high, and it cannot be successful without a larger value of resistance coupling. Therefore, resistance coupling is the best. Although the amplification rate of this type is limited to the vacuum tube itself when applied, and a high-value B voltage must be prepared, the emergence of pentode high-power output tubes and the circulation of AC power have also solved the problem.

Figure 3

It is commonly believed that in order to obtain greater output power, a push-pull connection using transformer coupling is necessary. However, this is not the case. Resistance coupling can also be used for push-pull amplification. Only one reverse-phase vacuum tube needs to be added, as shown in Figure 4·A. However, the voltage before and after this tube must be the same, otherwise distortion will occur.

Figure 4

(C) Mixed Resistance Coupling

This type of coupling method is quite similar to the aforementioned resistance coupling, as shown in Figure 5. The difference is that the change in the screen current of the front tube is transmitted to the voltage change of the grid of the rear tube, which does not pass through a resistor, but through the total impedance of inductance and capacitance in parallel. This type of coupling method is because its inductance impedance is larger than the differential resistance of the screen circuit, so the voltage amplification ratio will be equal to the amplification coefficient of the vacuum tube.

Figure 5

In order to obtain a higher voltage amplification ratio, mixed resistance coupling resistance coupling is better, because the first is because of the great [rest of the text is missing and garbled]

At the same time, the resistance is very small, so there is no need to apply a high voltage to the screen; second, the voltage input to the grid of the secondary tube is equal to the product of the screen current and the coupling resistance or impedance, and this type of coupling method, the total impedance after adding impedance to the screen circuit, is smaller than the total impedance of adding the same amount of resistance, so the screen current is larger, then the potential drop across the coupling impedance, that is, the voltage input to the rear tube is naturally higher, therefore this method is better than resistance coupling.

Figure 6 shows another type of mixed resistance coupling, called parallel screen voltage type, which is commonly used to avoid the magnetic field saturation of transformer coupling, and its effect is very good. Since it is mixed resistance coupling, it also does not lose the advantages of transformer coupling, commonly using resistors to replace low-frequency choke coils, which varies according to the design.

In addition, there is also a direct coupling type, but because it is less commonly used and more complicated, it will not be repeated.

Figure 6

Import of Wireless Materials This Year

Because my country's industry and commerce are immature, most of the wireless materials still rely on imports. The import volume this year has increased significantly compared with last year. According to foreign reports, the following is the situation.

In the first ten months of this year, the total value of wireless machines and parts imported into China was 1,348,400 yuan for American goods, 197,022 yuan for Japanese goods, 142,340 yuan for German goods, 108,856 yuan for British goods, 64,941 yuan for Dutch goods, and 36,397 yuan for other countries, totaling 1,898,158 yuan. Excluding 8,082 yuan returned to foreign countries, the total import volume was 1,890,076 yuan, which is equivalent to 3,723,669 yuan in national currency, an increase of more than 800,000 yuan compared with 2,936,035 yuan in the same period last year.

From this, it can be seen that if my country wants to promote the wireless industry, it still needs to work hard to manufacture its own components so as to reduce leakage.

Vacuum Tubes and Sound Quality

— Gu Yaoming

I made a four-tube AC machine myself, with 24 high-frequency amplification, 56 detection, 47 amplification, and 80 rectification. The speaker uses a dynamic type, and the parts are all suitable. After it was made, the sound quality was extremely poor, and the radio reception was blurry; using a pickup to play music, the sound quality was very good. This must be a high-frequency amplification problem. The inspection result was that the 24 tube had been shelved for too long, and I didn't test it when I bought it. There seemed to be an unnecessary gas leaking between the filament plate and the barrier electrode, turning into a blue light, resulting in blurry and poor sound quality. I once tested it, as shown in the figure, with B+ connected to the barrier electrode. Later I realized that vacuum tubes also have a close relationship with sound quality.

Simple Measurement Method for the Ratio of Audio Frequency Transformers

— Pao

There is a simple measurement method for the ratio of audio frequency transformers. The instruments used are nothing more than an AC voltmeter that can measure up to 45 volts, and an electric bell square shed (or replace it with a low-voltage coil of a power transformer). When measuring, first connect the primary of the electric bell square shed to the power line, and the secondary to the primary of the audio frequency transformer. Then use an AC voltmeter to measure the voltage of the secondary of the audio frequency transformer, and divide this number by the voltage of the secondary coil of the electric bell square shed to get the ratio of the audio frequency transformer. For example, if the voltage of the secondary coil of an audio frequency transformer is measured to be 15 volts according to the above method, and the secondary of the electric bell transformer used is 6 volts, dividing 15 by 6 yields a quotient of 2.5, so we know that the ratio of this audio frequency transformer is 2.5.

Difficulties and Remedies Commonly Encountered on Radios (Continued)

— Zhenmin

(5) Howling Noise (A stormy noise heard in the radio) Cause Remedy

(1) Storage battery power is exhausted Charge or replace

(2) B battery voltage is too high Find a way to reduce it (use a low-voltage battery or insert an appropriate resistor.)

(3) Poor resistors in the grid circuit Replace with better resistors.

(4) Magnetic induction between the squares Change their installation positions.

(5) Poor circuit insulation Inspect and repair.

(6) Scratchy Noise

Cause Remedy

(1) Grid leakage Replace the vacuum tube. Or find a way to make the contact tight.

(2) The soldering point is corroded by acid Re-solder.

(3) The contact between the vacuum tube bulb and the tube socket is incomplete Find a way to tighten it. (To be continued)

Free Talk

Dostoevsky, Shaw, and Pirandello

— Tianren

In Pirandello's eyes, the world is just a "lie". Everyone wears a mask, relying on "instinctive conscience" to live by telling "lies". Rational life laughs, but instinctive "life" secretly sheds tears. The author is troubled by real life. This is the case in "Six Characters in Search of an Author."

Starting from here, after he wrote "Come Prima, Meglio di Prima" (As Before, Better Than Before), his philosophy leaped even further, turning the "reality" and fiction in "Six Characters in Search of an Author" into fantasy.

Finally, even fantasy was not enough, so he brought out mad characters. The protagonist in "Henry IV" (Enrico IV) is such a character.

Real life annoyed the author. It goes without saying that the annoyance was caused by the doubt arising from the real society. What happens next? Satire, what else can be done? Other than satire, if you want to satirize, you have to make the half-crazy characters express themselves uncomfortably.

Pirandello's worldview is like this. First, compare him with Dostoevsky. They have something in common at the starting point of their creation.

Pirandello said that life is dualistic. There is "right" and "wrong" in life. Only the misery and unhappiness of human instincts can occur in a rational society. He looked at these with anger.

There is also an element of social injustice in Dostoevsky's realism. We can understand this by reading "Crime and Punishment". There is a "prophetic" element in Dostoevsky's works, but Pirandello always expresses "doubt" about life.

In "Henry IV", the protagonist is a Quixote. Everything in society is unpleasant to him, so he goes back to the eleventh century, puts on the costumes of ancient emperors, and lives like a lunatic. If he didn't doubt real life, would he need to go crazy? But in the end, he has to eat human food. One day, he fell off his horse, like a big dream, and dragged him back from a life of contradictions. He saw that his beloved lover had become someone else's wife. This made him angry again, and he went back to his madness, resulting in a bloody tragedy. This is another Quixote. He can't think of a way to solve reality, only doubt.

He said this in the short story Laprapcole:

"Some form of life is death. We only know that we are some trapped people. You can't always make him abandon us and head towards the road of death. Our existence has already been destined."

This is the sorrow of disillusionment caused by doubt. Can you say that he is the same as Dostoevsky?

There is also an element of humor, which is also very important in modern Italian literature. For example, Nanzini and Campanile, who were contemporaries of Pirandello, were called masters of humor, because they doubted the real society, so they wanted to appeal for injustice, stubbornly kick down reason, and find a way out for instinct. The protagonist often emits unhealthy satirical laughter from the tragedy, so humor is the best and only way.

Pirandello's humor is somewhat similar to Shaw's in his old age, but if you look closely, he is different from Shaw, but opposite to him.

Both of them are dissatisfied with the old society, and both deny the old social system with a satirical tone. Shaw's humor seems to have a critical meaning, while Pirandello's humor is just a mockery in the air. This is ultimately a "drawing a tiger" criticism. Humor that doesn't scratch the itch is even more mediocre and boring. What's the use of empty satire?

Some say that Shaw is "relying on his old age to sell his wisdom", but Pirandello is not much younger than him.

At Haiphong

— Li Qiao

After enduring half the night cramped in the cold train, Haiphong was finally in sight far away.

Towering buildings, sparkling bright lights, under the dark sky, the brilliance of thousands of electric lights reflected so red.

Far away, there was a vast expanse of white sea. The fields and temples shrouded in the night glowed with sparse lights. This late-night Haiphong was unexpectedly so beautiful and lovely, making the hearts of young people growing up in the countryside come alive.

In the paddy fields full of sparkling water, there were a few dim yellow electric lights bathing. I heard that this was used for fishing. This thing is really new.

After the car arrived in Haiphong, in the chaotic noise, I jumped into the car and was hurriedly pulled by a rickshaw driver to the shop, as if escaping.

Most of the shops here are opened by Cantonese people. Many overseas Chinese make a living here, but it's a pity that I don't understand Cantonese and can't talk to them about their living conditions. Only heaven knows.

The municipality of Haiphong is under the administration of French imperialism, and it is not bad: neat and clean asphalt roads are lined with rows of lush green trees. Walking slowly on this street under the hot sun during the day, people will not feel any heat.

Haiphong is the same as other cities: there is a park for people to visit. On the second day after arriving in Haiphong, having nothing to do, three young people made an appointment to go there for a walk.

Although the place is small, it is very quiet - tigers, leopards, etc. are all available. Several tropical plants, towering high, shaded the sky. Next to the flowerbeds with red and green reflections is a path paved with fine sand. With a curious heart, walking slowly on this road and admiring it, is quite interesting.

Because I had to wait for the ship, I couldn't help but delay the days. Every day when I got up, looking at the clear blue sky, the slowly floating white clouds, and the dark green distant trees, the heart of homesickness was drawn up by the scenery of this foreign country.

One morning, with tears in my eyes, I wrote a short letter to my father far away. I told him that I had quietly left him and ran to this foreign country. Please forgive me: I cannot help him with the hoe at home. I am a pursuer of light, and I want to go to the distant side of the sea!

Coarse Cloth

— TK

Returning from the Volcano (2)

— Lanru

With great difficulty, I endured the suffering until one o'clock. Because the wind and waves were too strong, the ship was like a flying machine suspended in the sky, sometimes rising from the seabed to the sky, and sometimes plummeting from the sky to the seabed. Neither Yang nor I could sleep, and our heads throbbed as if being hammered with iron. We both vomited violently, and I regretted coming. The suffering from Shanghai to Kobe had been enough, so why did I have to endure this pain again? I watched as the Japanese passengers slept soundly, snoring, while I stood alone on the stern, vomiting into the vast sea. At that moment, I further confirmed my view of life. Yes, life is painful, and also contradictory. We know full well that only through many difficulties and much suffering can we gain a moment of joy, yet we are willing to strive to pursue it desperately. I don't know if this is life's contradiction or life's true meaning? Is it the cleverness of human intelligence or its foolishness?

"We're here! We're here!"

In the vast darkness, we suddenly spotted electric lights flickering like stars. This was Ōshima Island. We felt joyful and excited, as if saved from death. The passengers all stood by the ship's railing, but as the wind and waves grew stronger, they squeezed back inside. However, I, greedy for the sight of the marine scenery heralding the dawn, forgot about the assault of the morning breeze, and my hands were already frozen.

Originally, the ship should have docked at Motomura, but because of the strong wind and waves, it couldn't. We had to change course and dock at Okada Port. The innkeepers, each carrying a lantern, lined up on the shore, calling out words of welcome to the guests. But no one wanted to go to the inn to rest, and everyone hurried onto the mountain ridge, bathed in the fish-belly-colored dawn.

From the foot of the mountain to the mountainside, you could take a car, and it only cost thirty cents. However, Mr. Qin suggested that walking would allow us to enjoy the scenery, and everyone agreed. At that time, three Japanese students from Tokyo Imperial University joined our group. One of them was acquainted with Mr. Qin, and this was his second time visiting the volcano, so he was a good guide for us. Like a group of soldiers on an expedition, we ran forward with vigor, eager to reach the summit as soon as possible and see the volcano, which we had never seen before, and to pay our respects to the nameless heroes who had committed suicide for love.

We took a different mountain path from the cars. Although there were no red leaves, the lush forests were as beautiful as spring. Bright red camellias bloomed everywhere, and the spring breeze gently blew on the faces of the visitors, creating an indescribable sense of comfort and warmth.

After walking more than six miles, our legs were a little sore, and our hunger was unbearable. So we sat down on the ground and ate the bread, fruit, and biscuits that each of us had brought. The three Imperial University students were more experienced than us after all, and had bought many cans of food and pork. We all put aside our own food and ate the meat they brought. Mr. Qin (a Japanese, our Japanese teacher) said with a smile, "Are you all carnivores?" In fact, he didn't understand that the Chinese are different from the Japanese. Even wealthy Japanese rarely eat meat, while the Chinese treat meat as a side dish.

Who Can Satisfy Their Material Needs?

— Bo Han

"If we want to eliminate that kind of spiritual superstition, we can only do so by satisfying their material needs. Whoever can satisfy the peasants' demands for harvest will be the one who can eliminate the superstition of 'harvest' among the peasants. Whoever can satisfy the material needs of the townspeople for a secure and happy life will be the one who can fundamentally eliminate superstition in the city." This is Mr. Wu Jian's conclusion in the "Free Talk" of December 3rd, discussing superstition.

Naturally, superstition cannot be eliminated by popular science lectures, nor by so-called superficial actions such as destroying temples, which are carried out from a position of social science. "Regarding superstition, the most important thing is to see its material origins." No one can make the farmers harvest more grain, so the farmers respect the Land God; no one can make the townspeople live in peace and happiness, so the city residents believe in the City God Bodhisattva. In other words, the so-called material origin is that the failure to satisfy material needs becomes the ultimate cause of superstition.

If human society one day realizes "human determination conquers nature" and material needs can be universally and rationally satisfied, then there should be no superstition at all. But now it is impossible to talk about the realization of "human determination conquers nature" in the whole society. If the material needs of some people are satisfied, superstition can be eliminated, then capitalists should not believe in God, and defeated warlords should not burn incense and chant Buddha.

Sometimes, it is precisely the satisfaction of material needs that consolidates the psychology of superstition. For example, if a poor person wins money in a lottery or wins the top prize in an aviation lottery, he will attribute it to the help of his deceased ancestors in the netherworld, or to the manifestation of a certain god he has prayed to in the past. In the present, when mankind does not universally enjoy happiness, the satisfaction and dissatisfaction of the material needs of some people can often become the cause of superstition: because the point is not whether they are satisfied or not, but that the reasons for making people satisfied or dissatisfied are a blind, uncontrollable supernatural power for them.

However, in fact, for most people, who can satisfy their material needs? It is impossible for ordinary people of flesh and blood to shoulder this responsibility with individual strength. This can only rely on the power of society, that is, the power of the group, and must include themselves. If they do not grasp this point, but only pray to any savior other than themselves, whether it is a heavenly or earthly saint, if this mentality is not changed for a day, that is, if there is no self-confidence in their minds for a day, how can the root of superstition be eliminated?

Therefore, after talking about "starting from the contradictions of superstition itself," it seems that the contradiction between "who" and "them" in that conclusion should also be resolved.

Cocoon (2)

— (Original by Lin Fang) Translated by Jingzi

That's how it was.

This was one of the bad tempers of middle school students at that time. Senior students often bullied junior students. Using any unreasonable reason, they often liked to wave their barbaric fists at the pitiful victims in the deserted grassland. One day, when the two of us were taking a walk in the back mountain as usual, we were unexpectedly caught by that group of bad students.

One of them – always the son of the old boss of the local silk factory, that barbarian king who repeated grades, named Dahe – slowly approached.

"Ah, it's Sakai! You look really smug lately!"

Sakai stared at the other person's face for a while, and then resolutely said:

"How am I smug!"

The other party suddenly reached out and punched him in the chest.

"You junior, what are you being stubborn about! That's what I call smug!"

He fell to the ground, but soon got up again and punched the other party in the chest. However, his body was too small, and there were three people on the other side, so he was finally knocked down to the ground again, and beaten wildly like a puppy. The second time he got up, this time he was holding a shiny new pencil sharpener in his right hand.

The color immediately disappeared from the other party's lips, and Sakai's cheeks suddenly turned pale. He chased after Dahe, who was scurrying like a rat.

The other party fled to the hill, which was the hill where Sakai had stepped on the snake's head before. The road had come to an end, and the other party, in the state of a cornered rat, turned back and stood there.

"If you have the guts to kill, then kill me and see!"

The other party, putting on a show of strength, took off his coat and threw it on the ground, stretching out his two trembling arms.

"I will kill you!"

Sakai's voice was listless. The cold light of the knife began to cut through the air.

"Ah!"

Watching from afar, all the blood in my body froze, and I involuntarily shouted out like this. And Dahe also fell to the ground at this time.

The group of companions hurried to lift Dahe's waist and ran forward. Sakai stared blankly, watching until the group disappeared into the woods. He inexplicably fell to the ground and didn't move.

My terrified soul recovered, and I hurried forward. His face was buried in the summer grass, and his eyebrows were twitching.

Why? I really don't understand why.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Conversations

Magazine Year and the Ancient Book Craze

— Rong

If this year is said to be the year of magazines, then within this year of magazines, there is a rather special phenomenon, which is the craze for reprinting ancient books. First, the experienced Commercial Press took the lead by reprinting the Complete Library of the Four Treasuries on a large scale. For a time, various bookstores rose up like a storm, competing to follow suit. Following this were the Zhonghua Book Company's Illustrated Compendium of Books, the Kaiming Bookstore's Twenty-Five Histories, and the Book and Newspaper Cooperative's Twenty-Six Histories, and the Commercial Press's Ten Comprehensive Records. These were all amazing projects. Those compiled and printed by private individuals also included the recently reported Collection of Ci Poetry and Prose. Ancient books, which had been suppressed for many years, can be said to be having a great run of luck lately. However, when we look back at the garden of new culture, even single-volume creations are withering away badly. Publishers are vying to take the path of magazines. Although there are many magazines, when compared with the reprinted ancient books, the human and financial resources spent are much smaller and more pitiful. This is a distorted development, and this distorted development has deep-rooted social relations.

In short, we are not opposed to receiving past heritage and sorting out past heritage. However, the question is how to do the work of receiving and sorting out, and what are the motives and ultimate goals of this work? The evolution of human society, in addition to the biological inheritance of individuals, also has cultural inheritance, because culture progresses by accumulation. Therefore, modern culture can hardly be isolated from past culture. However, the so-called receiving heritage means searching and sorting out things that are beneficial to the development of modern culture from the past heritage with a critical eye, because its starting point and ultimate goal are in the creation of new culture, so it is very different from the general reversal of history and blind adherence to ancient ways. Although the methods of the Ten Comprehensive Records, Twenty-Five Histories, etc. are old, they can help us understand the past society. The Collection of Ci Poetry and Prose may also provide us with materials for studying ancient literary criticism. In a sense, this is very gratifying. However, whether publishers are consciously doing this now is still a question. Otherwise, why spend heavily to reprint dozens or even hundreds of "masterpieces," but not be willing to take a fraction of this capital to print some small pamphlets and single volumes that are not easy to profit from but are very beneficial to the general readers? Ancient books do not have their own independent value. Ancient books only have their value in promoting the growth of new books. In other words, reprinting ancient books is only a means of promoting culture, not an end. It is only valuable to reprint ancient books for the sake of new books.

However, when we look at the new books in recent years, single volumes have been very few, and only magazines are supporting the scene. Are there no new works worth printing as single volumes? Just saving two glass plates for reprinting ancient books, and reducing some icing on the cake in terms of decoration, wouldn't the money saved be enough to print two new works that are very readable? Publishers should not produce purely for the purpose of "making profit."

The problem falls on the readers. You are not willing to reverse the trend of history and pursue the dream of restoring the past, and your desire for knowledge is extremely strong. In this environment, what should you do? The pyramids of Memphis appear as rose-colored pillars in the morning light, but show black triangular shadows in the afterglow. A thing often has two sides, advantages and disadvantages. As long as you are willing to work hard, you will not find it difficult to sift out the glittering gold grains of new knowledge from the sand of ancient books!

Words of the Bookworm

— Rong

Whenever the sun sets and I walk to that newly opened French bookstore on Nanjing Road with a slightly casual mood, I am often attracted by the colorful and beautiful covers in the glass window. I smoke and put my hands in the pockets of my coat, unwilling to leave. The urban street scene of busy traffic behind me has long been forgotten, and my fantasy is wandering in the poetic realm of Verlaine and Baudelaire. I don't have any money, so I just stare at those small books in a daze. Even when I leave, my steps are doubly slow, and I look back with a little reluctance and melancholy at the neon lights that have just been lit.

I am passionate about reading books, ancient, modern, Chinese, Western, thirty-two-mo sized, sixteen-mo sized, thread-bound, leather-bound, I am willing to collect them all. As long as I open a newly bought book and smell the scent of the paper, I yearn to browse through it with a feeling of excitement and gratitude. As long as I go to a bookstore and see the books taking various poses and wearing various clothes, leaning on the bookshelves, I really want to transplant each one to my small study. In the morning or at dusk, I want to madly drink the wisdom of the times by the dim light of the sun and the glow of the bright lamp.

However, this wish is very difficult to achieve after all. It is just as the Greek myth says, a person is punished by the gods, forever able to see the鲜艳 of the apple and smell the芬香 of the apple, but unable to quickly enjoy it. This is an unbearable punishment. When I don't have money, I sometimes go to old bookstores to play around. There are many bookstores on North Sichuan Road and the City God Temple. Every one opens its doors for you to enter. Just searching and discovering in this is an indescribable pleasure, like walking into the Shanyin Road, with no time to take it all in. On this side is a verdant and lush cliff, and on that side are several clusters of beautiful mountain flowers, and even streams and thatched huts. As long as you are patient, you will not find it difficult to discover them one by one. Even if you don't return满载而归, isn't that翻阅 also give you奇趣 that movie theaters and dance halls cannot provide?

France said: "Books are the opium of the West, they will destroy us." This of course means that reading becomes so engrossed in and uncontrolled that one sinks into a chronic suicide, but the choice and discernment are also up to ourselves, and opium can sometimes be used as a medicinal material. An author uses his wisdom to write a book, and this book is displayed on the bookshelves of many people. His name is constantly being mentioned, and his ideas affect the ideas of countless people. He is no longer himself, he has merged with the souls of many readers. And a reader can make some good friends from the black words on white paper and peek at the familiar faces of each of them.

As for me, I like to read books that are rich in nourishment, which makes my skeleton healthy and my muscles plump, so I often spend my spare time on this. A cup of tea, a Peace cigarette, whether you lean on it to watch or sit to read, this aftertaste is sweet enough.

If the bookworm erodes books, or erodes books because it loves books, then I am willing to be a bookworm, but not a bookworm that desperately, indomitably, and painstakingly studies, but a bookworm that can wander in the縹緗, eat the book, and digest the book!

Winter Storage

— Forget Myself

Home

— Hu Weixiong

In winter, the sky is filled with heavy fog. Dragging my tired body and the suitcase that has suffered the wind and frost for a year, I go to the train station.

There are unexpectedly many passengers at the station, carrying big bags and small suitcases, probably all stealing a few days of vacation to return to their homes. I squeezed out of the crowd onto the platform, and after occupying a seat in the carriage, the train slowly left the station.

Naturally, the carriage is equally crowded with people, all of whom have tired bodies, but I also know that the joy in their hearts is the same as mine. The joy of wanderers being able to return to their hometowns at the so-called end of the year can be imagined. Thinking that a week ago, I received a letter written by my child, who was learning to write, I turned the calendar to calculate the date of returning home, and even became lazy at work. Originally, having been away from home for six or seven years, I just wrote a family letter at the end of each year. Now that the child in his mother's arms can pick up a pen and write a letter asking his father to come home, thinking about those long and distant days, how can it not excite people?

Last night, I received double my salary from the account room's window. When I walked out of the factory gate, I felt like a big rich man. Walking through the bustling street, I was sometimes mesmerized by the neon lights in the glass cabinets. I should cut a nice piece of clothing material for my wife and buy a beautiful hat for my six or seven year old child. But paying attention to the prices marked on them, I felt that my double salary seemed too small. So I went from this bustling street to that one, and picked out objects that suited me in many, many glass cabinets. When I returned to my residence, I carefully put them into my suitcase, anticipating the unexpected joy that these gifts would receive.

When I get to the door of my house, my child must be waiting at the door, but I don't recognize him, and he doesn't recognize me. So I will go up and ask him my name. I can clearly hear from his small mouth; "That's my dad." I will pick him up, kiss his apple-like face, and at the same time, my wife will hear my voice, put down the work in her hands, and run to the door to greet me.

When I get inside, perhaps my wife has specially prepared a snack for me. I will order the mother and son to close their eyes, and take out the gifts from the suitcase. The child is afraid of peeking at my movements, and when he sees the beautiful hat, he jumps up and snatches it away. When my wife sees the clothing material, she will also hold it up to the mirror and pose, just like when she was a new bride. How long has she not worn such expensive clothing material!

Thinking, thinking, just as I closed my eyes, I heard the rooster crow. And the alarm clock on the head of the bed, because I forgot to tighten the spring last night, the hour and minute hands stopped at twelve o'clock. At times like this, I hope that the death-urging whistle of the汔笛 will pull a long ring to estimate the time. But today this world is still, the factory gates are tightly closed, no smoke is rising from the chimney, and the companions who get up at that time every day are probably all in sweet dreams. Even the sparrows that chirp on the eaves are driven away by the heavy fog. If I can represent this world, it is my excited heart.

After the car started moving, it slowly calmed down. Naturally, in a short time, I can embrace my嬌妻 and撫愛子 and enjoy a family reunion.

When I take the bread out of my suitcase to fill my stomach, I also play with those two lovely gifts. In this way, the car will take me to my hometown.

Stepping on the land of my hometown, the scenery in front of me is all亲切. Having been separated from my hometown for six or seven years, I can still live to return. I am so happy that I am crying. But won't these few days of happy reunion pass in an instant? We are the pitiable people oppressed by life, as if we should not have a hometown or a family. Haven't we been tortured by life for six or seven years? Thinking like this, I can't help but slow down my steps. I'm afraid to see my door, and I don't know how my idealized嬌妻愛子 have been honed to. We are all human beings, why is there such inequality? The excited heart just now is now oppressed like today's heavy fog! However, the door of my house is finally getting closer and closer and is right in front of me...

Dusk

— Xue Hong

Dusk routinely crept into this spacious old mansion.

The electric lights were hung sparsely, as if they were quietly peeking at something. All sorts of different postures were being displayed here, but in short, the atmosphere in this old mansion did not lose its peaceful order due to the activities of many individuals.

The teachers were not hiding in their bedrooms smoking cigarettes because they were correcting homework, but were sitting on the edge of the bed in groups of three or four, talking about something that others could not join in. There were no people going to the street to visit friends or stroll around tonight, probably because no one initiated it.

The teachers' affairs, the students don't need to know, and the students' affairs, the teachers don't need to know, this seems to be what every student is asking for in their hearts. In fact,

Page 23

there is no need to ask, but what is desired has already been realized. Because various possible techniques are sufficient to make it impossible for teachers to know all the things that students like to do that should be prohibited. However, perhaps some teachers clearly know something about the students but pretend to be deaf and dumb.

In this way, under the light intensity that connects brightness and darkness, in the corners of the wall suitable for private conversations, some people dare to whisper secrets.

"I'm not afraid of people saying bad things about me. Aren't young people worthy of being in love?"

With pursed lips and glancing eyes, it was clearly the tone of a reckless child.

"Who says young people aren't worthy of being in love!"

He placed his two palms on the head of his young companion, making a proud and joyful pose. The person looked only seventeen or eighteen years old.

"Let me see her letter!" The companion demanded from him.

A pink letter was slowly and carefully pulled out from the child's uniform pants pocket.

The companion took it and read aloud the salutation at the beginning of the letter.

"How can you read it out loud!" The child snatched it back and stuffed it into his pocket, saying seriously, "She really loves me!"

He said that she was like a devil, not knowing how to suppress the burning passion that was about to rush out of her heart. He also said how infatuatedly he stared at her in the classroom, making all the teacher's lectures muddled, when she occasionally turned her face back and smiled at him. He also said how he often wanted to make an appointment with her for a happy date at an appropriate time. Finally, he also said that his mood lately was so irritable and depressed. Compared with when he usually saw what he loved toys or candy, there was a clear difference. That is, the desire for toys or candy could be immediately satisfied or eliminated, but now it could not be done immediately, and something like a snake was entrenched in his chest, feeling strangely suffocated.

"Confess it all!" The young man, sensing the surging emotions of the other party with his own burning eyes, said with sympathy and ridicule, "I'm very good at helping you think of a way, Old Wang has a lot of skills!"

Seeing Old Wang patting his chest, knowing that his happiness was at hand, the child bravely said, without any hesitation:

"Really? Don't mess around! I want to ask her to see a movie."

"Then just write another letter," Old Wang said with certainty.

"I'm just afraid she won't come out."

"Who said she won't come out?" A third voice suddenly came from behind.

The two young people turned their heads at the same time, and a classmate stuck out his tongue and made a face at the dean of students who came from the darkness.

Year-End Signals

— Bei

Time truly flies; after several urgent gusts of the old northerly wind, the year-end is almost upon us. According to past conventions, the period around the year-end is always very lively. This isn't to say that officials are busy acquiring properties, wealthy people are busy enjoying themselves, candy stores on Nanjing Road are packed with customers, dance halls and movie theaters are bustling until dawn, and everything is filled with laughter and excitement; rather, it refers to the universal clamor of pleading for loans, the fierce demands of debt collectors, the busy slaughtering of pigs on the streets, the frequent occurrence of thefts, and the tragedies and bloody incidents that arise from these.

Indeed, as the year-end approaches, while many people are cheering and singing wildly, many others are left in a state of mixed emotions, unsure whether to laugh or cry. It is a time of joy, but also a season of sorrow. Especially in a metropolis like this, the year-end is marked only by chaos, chaos, and more chaos. Our school cannot escape this fate either, as recent events powerfully demonstrate. This suddenly made me realize, alas, the year-end is here!

This isn't just my bad luck and financial loss; it's a reflection of the poverty of society. However, the unfolding of the facts has left me with a belly full of anger that I cannot vent. I haven't neglected my defenses; I always tell the school workers to be vigilant because thefts frequently occur in the school. Before going to the office, I always carefully close the windows and lock the doors. With such "precautions" in place, I shouldn't have to worry too much about my belongings in the room. Besides, I'm used to being casual, and my clothes are always "thrown around," tossed in corners, hung on walls, piled on the bed. At a glance, the room seems full of clothes, but there aren't really that many, and most of them are old and useless. Just recently, I made a huge decision—it took a lot of effort—to save up some money and make two suits. Because I usually wear tattered old clothes, having brand new suits, especially Western suits, naturally makes me value them immensely. Precisely because of this, I suppressed the urge to wear them, hanging them on the wall, looking at them from time to time, as if just looking at them satisfied my craving to wear them. Enough. That pair of Hailing pen brand suits, I've really only worn them twice; they're practically brand new.

The little thief who specializes in taking care of me really has sharp eyes, constantly watching me. Last time, he stole my fur coat, and now he's come to steal my suit. It's not that I neglected things, but my door lock isn't very secure. He took advantage of my absence at the office, and very calmly (I imagine he was very calm) picked my lock and walked away with my suit.

Good heavens, this really infuriated me; the suit was brand new!

However, this isn't just my bad luck and financial loss; it's a reflection of the poverty of society, or at least a common occurrence in a capitalist society like Shanghai, or at least an inevitable symptom in schools under the current education system. As the year-end approaches, theft has become a general trend of the season. In the past week, many similar thefts have occurred here. One classmate had his clothes stolen, and the thief even left

Page 24

Page 25

behind a note to play a joke on him. It is said that these thieves have significant backing. One was caught, and the result of the interrogation was that he was a university student. Alas, university education is ruined.

As the year-end approaches, how chaotic this society is!

Amateur Mailbox

Questions About Recruiting Salespersons

Editor:

I am a young man who has been unemployed for a long time. I worked as a salesman in a paper store for three years. Recently, I saw an advertisement in your newspaper from a certain sales company recruiting salespersons. I made an appointment with a friend to take the test together. We filled out applications there, submitted photos, and were asked a few questions by their staff. Finally, they replied with the simple sentence, "Whether or not you are accepted will be notified in writing later."

A dozen days later, the company indeed sent a letter: "Our company has already started working on the sixteenth. Please report for duty immediately upon receiving this letter, and bring one yuan for the badge fee." It was just a few simple words like that.

The next morning, I brought the original letter and went to report for duty with my friend. But when we got there, we saw that there were quite a few people reporting for duty, about one or two hundred. In the end, the people in the company said, "The money has been collected first, but the badges have not yet been made." This made people very suspicious, and seeing that the company had nothing of value, just a few desks for decoration, I didn't report for duty.

Editor: You are the mentors of young people in the professional world. I now have three points of doubt, please answer them as follows:

(1) The company has no restrictions on recruiting salespersons. With so many unemployed people now, there must be a large number of applicants. Perhaps they are using this to collect money, which is not known.

(2) No one in the company is formally responsible. Those who greeted the applicants were all young people who looked like trainees, which clearly showed that there was no organization at all.

(3) The company is very dismissive of the guarantee issue and does not investigate it at all. With the heavy responsibility of a salesperson, not paying attention to this shows that they have other intentions.

The above three points are really doubts that I cannot resolve. I hope you will spare an hour and a half of your time to give me guidance so that I will not be deceived. If you think it is necessary, please publish it in the newspaper so that others can learn from it. A dollar for the unemployed is so important! Dear Sir: I am waiting for your reply! Wishing you

Well-being.

Respectfully, Wang Qiheng, November 21st

Editor's Note: Mr. Wang's letter did not specify the name and address of the sales company, so it seems impossible to investigate the truth. Moreover, the situation described is not clear, so the editor cannot rashly make a judgment. However, in Shanghai, which is outwardly prosperous but internally dark, there are many deceptive businesses, and there is a risk of being harmed if one is slightly negligent. Mr. Wang's careful consideration after discovering suspicious points about the sales company is the right thing to do. Unemployed people should carefully examine all recruitment agencies that have no credit guarantee and focus on collecting money from applicants to avoid being deceived.

As for the sales company, if it believes that the situation described by Mr. Wang needs to be supplemented, it can send a letter to clarify. The editor will announce it within the possible scope.

Boatman's Song

The Yangtze River flows eastward, endlessly, endlessly, big boats and small boats travel east and west, downstream, downstream, coming and going, the river is long, coming and going, the times are long, the morning sun shines, the river waves shine, the deep night bright moon reflects the sandbar, the silly poet praises the boatman's joy, who knows the boatman's sorrow and sorrow.

The boatman's life depends on drifting, drifting, drifting, stopping endlessly east and west, upstream and downstream, busy when the cold and heat do not rest, idle when hunger is unbearable, paying taxes and no money to commit crimes, the family's life is pinned on a flat boat, sometimes encountering evil storms, the whole family will rest once.

Suzhou Ballad

China and West (1040) 11:45 PM to 12:30 AM

Opening "Resist Japanese Goods"

Fusang three islands are rampant. Looking at them greedily like tigers and wolves. The Twenty-One Demands are unreasonable. The intention is to invade our rights and seize our territory. In a few days, the Japanese dared to rob us. The Japanese are greedy and will not die, and their anger is even greater. Therefore, our people cannot bear it. They jointly planned to resist and came up with a long-term strategy. People from all walks of life have been dispatched to various places. Warn compatriots to work hard. Quickly recover the lost land. Unison singing is enthusiastic. It is pitiful that there is no way to appeal. Therefore, compatriots must resist imported goods. Cutting off his business is the best way. I am a small patriotic heart that has not died. Please listen carefully to a humble word. That is, perseverance, firmness and endurance. Don't be violent and cause discord. Never be enthusiastic for five minutes and then become cold. Being ridiculed and teased by foreigners is embarrassing. There is one more important thing. Improving domestic goods should be advocated first. We must know that the only way for a country to become rich is through industry. Everyone must do their best to help. If we can export high-quality goods that are better than Japanese goods. Cheap and beautiful, everyone praises it. If the source is cut off, there is no need to say more. Let him have trouble selling his goods and panic. The lost land will be recovered and the treaty will be destroyed. Compatriots have a good start and peace and health. Otherwise, it is empty words to resist and the call is urgent. Instead, the revival of domestic goods is put aside. If there is no way to get it, buy Western goods. Isn't it resisting Japanese goods and entering the West? Profits are still lost and the fat is exhausted. "Korea's example is inevitable to perish. I hope you will carefully consider this statement. I can comfort my writing of this long article.
